#СТК#
RSS_STK_decisions = {
	RSS_STK_credit_coop = {
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 70
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = {  
			NOT = { has_government = despotism }
			NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
		}
		modifier = {
			consumer_goods_factor = -0.03
		}
		complete_effect = {}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	RSS_STK_new_tech = {
		cost = 150
		days_remove = 120
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = {  
			check_variable = { stability > 0.34 } 
			NOT = { has_government = despotism }
			NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
		}
		modifier = {
			production_factory_efficiency_gain_factor = 0.06
		}
		complete_effect = {}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	RSS_STK_reform_non_effective ={
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 70
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = {
			NOT = { has_government = despotism }
			NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
		}
		modifier = {
			production_factory_start_efficiency_factor = 0.05
		}
		complete_effect = {}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	RSS_STK_more_plants = {
		cost = 120
		days_remove = 70
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = {  
			NOT = { has_government = despotism }
			NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
		}
		modifier = {
			production_speed_industrial_complex_factor = 0.06
		}
		complete_effect = {}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	RSS_STK_new_orders = {
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 70
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = {
			NOT = { has_government = despotism }
			NOT = { has_government = authoritarism }
		}
		modifier = {
			industrial_capacity_factory = 0.06
			civilian_factory_use = 2
		}
		complete_effect = {}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
	RSS_STK_close = {
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 35
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = { 
			OR = { 
				has_stability < 0.3  
				OR = { 
					has_government = despotism 
					has_government = social_conservatism 
					has_government = authoritarism 
					has_government = national_syndicalism 
					has_government = fascism 
				} 
			} 
		}
		visible = {
			OR = { 
				has_stability < 0.3  
				OR = { 
					has_government = despotism 
					has_government = social_conservatism 
					has_government = authoritarism 
					has_government = national_syndicalism 
				} 
			} 
		}
		modifier = {}
		remove_effect = { 
			clr_country_flag = RSS_STK_open 
			remove_ideas = RSS_STK
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	RSS_establish_gg_in_non_core_234 = {
	
		icon = generic_political_discourse
		
		visible = {
			OR = {
				original_tag = RSS
				AND = {
					
					
				}
			}
			234 = {
				is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT
				OR = { is_core_of = RUS is_core_of = UKR }
				NOT = { is_core_of = ROOT }
			}
		}
	
		cost = 10
		days_remove = 7
		
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 234 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1000
			modifier = {
				add = 10
				divisions_in_state = {
					size < 1
					state = 234
				}
				234 = {
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT } }
				}
			}
		}
		
		remove_effect = {
			234 = {
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}
			907 = {
				add_core_of = ROOT
			}

				add_core_of = ROOT
			}

#Резервный фронт
RSS_reserve_front = {
	drop_reverse_front = {
		cost = 0
		days_remove = 21
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = { surrender_progress > 0.39 }
		complete_effect = {
			hidden_effect = {
				load_oob = RSS_reserve_front_oob
			}
			custom_effect_tooltip = RSS_reserve_front_effect
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

#Координация восстаний
RSS_coord_uprisings_decisions = {
	
	RSS_uprising_in_state_213 = {
	
		icon = generic_civil_support
		available = {
			ROOT = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 499 } }
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = RSS
			
			213 = {
				NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
				CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = RSS }
				NOT = { has_state_flag = eser_rebels_called }
				any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = RSS } }
				any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { NOT = { tag = RGR } } }
				any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = RSS }
			}
		}
	
		cost = 35
		days_remove = 14
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 213 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size > 4
					state = 213
				}
				213 = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			
			213 = {
				save_global_event_target_as = state_var 
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = RSS_eser_uprising
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:state_var = { NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT } } 
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = -500
					}
					event_target:state_var = { 
						spawn_eser_rebels_script = yes 
						set_state_flag = eser_rebels_called
						hidden_effect = {
							state_event = { id = rss_eser_tech.4 days = 364 }
						}
					}
					clear_global_event_target = state_var
				}
				else = { add_political_power = 35 }	
			}
		}
	}

			ROOT = { has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 499 } }
		}
		
		visible = {
			original_tag = RSS
			
			
			242 = {
				NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT }
				CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = RSS }
				NOT = { has_state_flag = eser_rebels_called }
				any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = RSS } }
					any_neighbor_state = { CONTROLLER = { NOT = { tag = RGR } } }
				any_neighbor_state = { is_controlled_by = RSS }
			}
		}
	
		cost = 35
		days_remove = 14
		highlight_state_targets = { state = 242 }
		
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
			modifier = {
				add = 100
				divisions_in_state = {
					size > 4
					state = 242
				}
				242 = {
					CONTROLLER = { has_war_with = ROOT }
				}
			}
		}
		
		complete_effect = {
			
			242 = {
				save_global_event_target_as = state_var 
			}
		}
		remove_effect = {
			custom_effect_tooltip = RSS_eser_uprising
			hidden_effect = {
				if = {
					limit = {
						event_target:state_var = { NOT = { is_fully_controlled_by = ROOT } } 
					}
					add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
						type = infantry_equipment
						amount = -500
					}
					event_target:state_var = { 
						spawn_eser_rebels_script = yes 
						set_state_flag = eser_rebels_called
						hidden_effect = {
							state_event = { id = rss_eser_tech.4 days = 364 }
						}
					}
					clear_global_event_target = state_var
				}
				else = { add_political_power = 35 }	
			}
		}
	}

RSS_green_rebels_support = {
	green_rebel_support_RVA = {
		cost = 15
		days_remove = 14
		days_re_enable = 1
		available = { 
			has_equipment = { infantry_equipment > 699 }
		}
		visible = { 
			RSS = { has_war_with = RVA } 
			any_neighbor_country = { tag = RVA } 
		}
		remove_effect = {
			RVA = { add_stability = -0.03 }
			add_equipment_to_stockpile = {
				type = infantry_equipment
				amount = -700
			}
			add_to_variable = {
				var = global.RCW_green_var_Russian_volunteer_army
				value = 1
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 10
		}

#Конструктивный социализм
RSS_Chernov_book = {
	Chernov_writes_book = {
		cost = 100
		days_remove = 360
		fire_only_once = yes
		available = { 
			has_country_leader = {
				name = "Victor Chernov" 
				ruling_only = yes
			}	 
		}
		remove_effect = {
			if = {
				limit = { 
					has_country_leader = {
						name = "Victor Chernov" 
						ruling_only = yes
					}
				}
				add_country_leader_trait = a_living_classic_of_socialism
				news_event = { id = rss_eser_news.2 }
			}
		}
		ai_will_do = {
			factor = 1
		}
	}
}

	RSS_self_sorganization_of_BSK = {
		activation = { has_country_flag = RSS_autonomies_granted controls_state = 651 BSK = { exists = no } }
		available = {
			controls_state = 651
			BSK = { exists = no }
		}
		days_mission_timeout = 4
		timeout_effect = {
